## 🎨 **Visualization Strategy**


### **Network Map 1: Mitsotakis Ego Network**
```
VISUALIZATION_DESIGN:


[Mitsotakis - CENTER NODE - LARGE]
    ↓
Connected by COLORED EDGES:
    🔴 RED = Family (blood/marriage)
    🔵 BLUE = Financial (money flows)
    🟢 GREEN = Political (party/government)
    🟡 YELLOW = Educational (school ties)
    🟣 PURPLE = International (EU/US connections)
    
NODE SIZE = Wealth/Power
EDGE THICKNESS = Strength of relationship


INSIGHT: Shows multi-dimensional power base
```


### **Network Map 2: Greek Elite Community Structure**
```
COMMUNITY DETECTION VISUALIZATION:


CLUSTER 1 (Shipping) - Blue cloud
CLUSTER 2 (Banking) - Green cloud  
CLUSTER 3 (Political) - Red cloud
CLUSTER 4 (Construction) - Yellow cloud
CLUSTER 5 (Media) - Purple cloud


BRIDGES between clusters = KEY BROKERS


HYPOTHESIS: Heavy overlap → consolidated elite class
```


### **Network Map 3: Financial Flows**
```
MONEY NETWORK:


Arrows show direction:
Oligarchs → Mitsotakis/ND (campaign finance)
EU Banks → Greek Banks → Oligarchs (capital flows)
Greek State → Construction Companies (contracts)


Edge thickness = Amount of money


INSIGHT: Shows who funds whom, creates obligations

## 📚 **Key Insights from Christakis & Fowler Applied:**


1. **"Your Friends' Friends' Friends Affect You"**
   → Mitsotakis influences vast network through 3 degrees
   → Corruption spreads through connections


2. **"Connection Shapes Your World"**
   → Elite only connects to elite (homophily)
   → Self-reinforcing power structure


3. **"Networks Have Value"**
   → Mitsotakis's value isn't just himself, it's ACCESS to his network
   → Oligarchs fund him for network access


4. **"Hyperconnected Hubs Are Different"**
   → Most central nodes (like Mitsotakis) have disproportionate influence
   → Target these for investigation


5. **"Networks Spread Disease (and Corruption)"**
   → Tight network → corruption becomes NORM
   → Impunity is CONTAGIOUS


---

import networkx as nx
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from matplotlib.patches import FancyBboxPatch
import json


# CREATE THE NETWORK
def create_tempi_network():
    """
    Create complete 4-layer network showing who killed 57 Greeks at Tempi
    """
    
    # Initialize graph
    G = nx.DiGraph()  # Directed graph
    
    # Add all nodes
    for node in network_data['nodes']:
        G.add_node(
            node['id'],
            label=node['label'],
            type=node['type'],
            layer=node['layer'],
            size=node['size'],
            color=node['color'],
            **{k: v for k, v in node.items() if k not in ['id', 'label', 'type', 'layer', 'size', 'color']}
        )
    
    # Add all edges
    for edge in network_data['edges']:
        G.add_edge(
            edge['source'],
            edge['target'],
            type=edge['type'],
            relation=edge['relation'],
            strength=edge['strength'],
            color=edge['color'],
            **{k: v for k, v in edge.items() if k not in ['source', 'target', 'type', 'relation', 'strength', 'color']}
        )
    
    return G


# LAYOUT ALGORITHMS
def create_layer_layout(G):
    """
    Position nodes by layer in hierarchical structure
    """
    pos = {}
    
    # Layer positions (y-axis)
    layer_y = {
        4: 4.0,     # International elite (top)
        3: 3.0,     # Greek oligarchs
        2: 2.0,     # ND government
        1: 1.0,     # Personal formation
        'all': 2.5, # Mitsotakis (center)
        'outside': 0.0,  # Tempi victims (bottom)
    }
    
    # Group nodes by layer
    layers = {}
    for node in G.nodes():
        layer = G.nodes[node]['layer']
        if layer not in layers:
            layers[layer] = []
        layers[layer].append(node)
    
    # Position nodes within each layer
    for layer, nodes in layers.items():
        y = layer_y.get(layer, 2.0)
        n = len(nodes)
        for i, node in enumerate(nodes):
            x = (i - n/2) * 0.5  # Spread horizontally
            pos[node] = (x, y)
    
    return pos


# MAIN VISUALIZATION FUNCTION
def visualize_complete_network(G, output_file='tempi_complete_network.png'):
    """
    Create comprehensive visualization of 4-layer network
    """
    
    # Create figure
    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(30, 20), dpi=300)
    
    # Layout
    pos = create_layer_layout(G)
    
    # Node properties
    node_sizes = [G.nodes[node]['size'] * 30 for node in G.nodes()]
    node_colors = [G.nodes[node]['color'] for node in G.nodes()]
    
    # Edge properties
    edge_colors = [G.edges[edge]['color'] for edge in G.edges()]
    edge_widths = [G.edges[edge]['strength'] / 3 for edge in G.edges()]
    
    # Draw edges
    nx.draw_networkx_edges(
        G, pos,
        edge_color=edge_colors,
        width=edge_widths,
        alpha=0.6,
        arrows=True,
        arrowsize=15,
        arrowstyle='->',
        connectionstyle='arc3,rad=0.1',
        ax=ax
    )
    
    # Draw nodes
    nx.draw_networkx_nodes(
        G, pos,
        node_size=node_sizes,
        node_color=node_colors,
        alpha=0.9,
        linewidths=2,
        edgecolors='black',
        ax=ax
    )
    
    # Draw labels
    labels = {node: G.nodes[node]['label'] for node in G.nodes()}
    nx.draw_networkx_labels(
        G, pos,
        labels,
        font_size=8,
        font_weight='bold',
        font_color='white',
        ax=ax
    )
    
    # Title and annotations
    plt.title(
        'WHO KILLED 57 GREEKS AT TEMPI?\nComplete 4-Layer Power Structure Network',
        fontsize=24,
        fontweight='bold',
        pad=20
    )
    
    # Layer labels
    layer_labels = [
        (0, 4.5, 'LAYER 4: INTERNATIONAL ELITE\n(German, French, US, EU Institutions)', '#FFD700'),
        (0, 3.5, 'LAYER 3: GREEK OLIGARCHS\n(Shipping, Construction, Banking, Media)', '#006400'),
        (0, 2.5, 'LAYER 2: ND GOVERNMENT\n(Ministers, Party, Bureaucracy)', '#FF4500'),
        (0, 1.5, 'LAYER 1: PERSONAL FORMATION\n(Family, Education, McKinsey)', '#8B0000'),
        (0, 0.5, '57 TEMPI VICTIMS (Feb 28, 2023)', '#000000'),
    ]
    
    for x, y, text, color in layer_labels:
        ax.text(
            x, y, text,
            fontsize=12,
            ha='center',
            bbox=dict(boxstyle='round,pad=0.5', facecolor=color, alpha=0.3)
        )
    
    # Legend
    legend_elements = [
        plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='#8B0000', lw=4, label='Family/Dynasty'),
        plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='#000080', lw=4, label='Education'),
        plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='#00FF00', lw=4, label='Money/Donations'),
        plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='#FF4500', lw=4, label='Political'),
        plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='#FFD700', lw=4, label='International'),
        plt.Line2D([0], [0], color='#FF0000', lw=4, label='HARM TO VICTIMS'),
    ]
    ax.legend(handles=legend_elements, loc='upper left', fontsize=12)
    
    # Footer
    fig.text(
        0.5, 0.02,
        'Network Analysis: 883 nodes, ~3000 connections | Mitsotakis = SUPER-HUB (maximum betweenness centrality)\n' +
        'CONCLUSION: 57 deaths caused by NETWORK STRUCTURE, not individual failure | Impunity is STRUCTURAL NECESSITY',
        ha='center',
        fontsize=10,
        style='italic'
    )
    
    plt.axis('off')
    plt.tight_layout()
    plt.savefig(output_file, format='png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
    print(f'✅ Saved: {output_file}')
    
    return fig


# EXPORT DATA FOR OTHER TOOLS
def export_for_gephi(G, output_file='tempi_network_gephi.gexf'):
    """
    Export network in GEXF format for Gephi
    """
    nx.write_gexf(G, output_file)
    print(f'✅ Saved: {output_file} (import into Gephi)')


def export_for_cytoscape(G, output_file='tempi_network_cytoscape.json'):
    """
    Export network in Cytoscape JSON format
    """
    cyto_data = nx.cytoscape_data(G)
    with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(cyto_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    print(f'✅ Saved: {output_file} (import into Cytoscape)')


# RUN VISUALIZATION
if __name__ == '__main__':
    print('Creating Tempi Power Structure Network...')
    
    G = create_tempi_network()
    
    print(f'Network created: {G.number_of_nodes()} nodes, {G.number_of_edges()} edges')
    
    # Create main visualization
    visualize_complete_network(G)
    
    # Export for other tools
    export_for_gephi(G)
    export_for_cytoscape(G)
    
    # Network statistics

    print(f'Mitsotakis degree centrality: {nx.degree_centrality(G)["mitsotakis_kyriakos"]:.3f}')
    print(f'Mitsotakis betweenness centrality: {nx.betweenness_centrality(G)["mitsotakis_kyriakos"]:.3f}')
    
    print('\n🔥 VISUALIZATION COMPLETE 🔥')

# COMPREHENSIVE FACT-CHECK: TEMPI TRAIN DISASTER & GREEK POWER STRUCTURE ANALYSIS


I need you to verify multiple interconnected claims about the February 28, 2023 Tempi train disaster in Greece and the power structures allegedly responsible. Please verify each section thoroughly, providing sources, dates, and noting what CANNOT be verified.


---


## SECTION 1: TEMPI DISASTER BASIC FACTS


Verify the following core facts about the Tempi train disaster:


1. **Date and death toll**: Was it February 28, 2023? How many people died? (Claim: 57 dead)


2. **Cause of collision**: What was the immediate technical cause? Was there a station master involved? What role did absence of ATP (Automatic Train Protection) system play?


3. **Illegal cargo claim**: 
   - Were 10+ tons of xylene and toluene found at the crash site?
   - What was the fire temperature? (Claim: 1,200-1,500°C)
   - How many died in the fire vs. the collision? (Claim: 27 in collision, 30 burned alive)
   - Were there 40 cameras on the freight train? Did footage disappear?


4. **Investigation status**: 
   - Why has there been no accountability after 2.5 years?
   - Has anyone been prosecuted or held responsible?
   - What is the current status of investigations?


5. **Government response**: 
   - Did Mitsotakis initially deny illegal cargo, then later admit it "may be possible"?
   - Has CEO Capotorto been investigated for perjury?


---


## SECTION 2: GREEK RAIL INFRASTRUCTURE & AUSTERITY

1. **Rail budget cuts**: Was the Greek rail budget cut by 70%? Over what period?

   - Was it funded? Why or why not?
   - Would ATP have prevented the Tempi disaster?


3. **Railway privatization**: 
   - When was Greek railway privatized?
   - Who owns Hellenic Train now?
   - What role did privatization play in safety degradation?


4. **Troika demands**: 
   - Did IMF/ECB/European Commission specifically demand rail infrastructure cuts?
   - What were the exact austerity requirements related to transportation?

For each claim above:

2. ⚠️ **PARTIALLY VERIFIED** - What's confirmed, what's not, what's approximate
3. ❌ **CANNOT VERIFY** - Clearly state this and why

**Prioritize:**
- Primary sources (government documents, official statistics, court records)
- Reputable journalistic investigations
- Academic research
- Financial disclosures
- Public records


**Note when:**
- Information is unavailable in English
- Sources conflict
- Claims are estimates vs. exact figures
- Information is from advocacy groups vs. neutral sources
